  19. I've had many pairs of nail clippers over the years, and Clyppi is much higher quality than any of them. That being said, Clyppi still has some issues.<br /><br />PROS:<br />- Compared to any other nail clippers I've used, Clyppi requires far less force to clip through a nail. This is the best thing about Clyppi.<br />- The blades are very sharp. They don't show any signs of dulling after clipping all fingernails and toenails ~10 times.<br /><br />CONS:<br />- The angle between the base and the lever is greater than that of any other clippers I've used. This makes it slightly awkward to hold. My thumb tends to slide down the lever because of the angle.<br />- It's possible for the lever to fall out of alignment with the pin that attaches it to the base, but only when the lever is flipped over in a very particular way (i.e. when the lever is inverted prior to storage of the clipper). When this happens, the lever gets jammed and the clipper is essentially broken. It can be fixed by popping the lever back into alignment, but this is rather difficult to do. (Suggestion to whoever designed Clyppi: make the hole in the lever fit more snugly with the pin.)
